          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Precondition: bulk-pinning is enabled.



<span class="line"><!---->Precondition: bulk-pinning is enabled.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When deleting a directory recursively in DriveFS, function drive::internal::DeleteOperation::Delete will post a task to UI thread from IO thread. The task has a bound raw pointer to PinManager [0].



<span class="line"><!---->When deleting a directory recursively in DriveFS, function drive::internal::DeleteOperation::Delete will post a task to UI thread from IO thread. The task has a bound raw pointer to PinManager [0].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





void Delete() {



<span class="line"><!---->void Delete() {<!----></span>



<br>





  base::File::Error error = base::DeletePathRecursively(path_)



<span class="line"><!---->  base::File::Error error = base::DeletePathRecursively(path_)<!----></span>



<br>





                                ? base::File::FILE_OK



<span class="line"><!---->                                ? base::File::FILE_OK<!----></span>



<br>





                                : base::File::FILE_ERROR_FAILED;



<span class="line"><!---->                                : base::File::FILE_ERROR_FAILED;<!----></span>



<br>





  if (error == base::File::FILE_OK && drive_) {



<span class="line"><!---->  if (error == base::File::FILE_OK &amp;&amp; drive_) {<!----></span>



<br>





    using drivefs::pinning::PinManager;



<span class="line"><!---->    using drivefs::pinning::PinManager;<!----></span>



<br>





    if (PinManager* const pin_manager = drive_->GetPinManager()) {



<span class="line"><!---->    if (PinManager* const pin_manager = drive_-&gt;GetPinManager()) {<!----></span>



<br>





      // TODO



<span class="line"><!---->      // TODO<!----></span>





(



<span class="line"><!---->(<!----></span>





b/267225898



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://b/267225898"><!---->b/267225898<!----></a>





): Local delete events are currently not sent via



<span class="line"><!---->): Local delete events are currently not sent via<!----></span>



<br>





      // DriveFS, so for now notify the `PinManager` for local deletes.



<span class="line"><!---->      // DriveFS, so for now notify the `PinManager` for local deletes.<!----></span>



<br>





      content::GetUIThreadTaskRunner({})->PostTask(          // <---- [0]



<span class="line"><!---->      content::GetUIThreadTaskRunner({})-&gt;PostTask(          // &lt;---- [0]<!----></span>



<br>





          FROM_HERE, base::BindOnce(&PinManager::NotifyDelete,



<span class="line"><!---->          FROM_HERE, base::BindOnce(&amp;PinManager::NotifyDelete,<!----></span>



<br>





                                    base::Unretained(pin_manager),



<span class="line"><!---->                                    base::Unretained(pin_manager),<!----></span>



<br>





                                    PinManager::Id(stable_id_), drive_path_));



<span class="line"><!---->                                    PinManager::Id(stable_id_), drive_path_));<!----></span>



<br>





    }



<span class="line"><!---->    }<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  ...



<span class="line"><!---->  ...<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/drive/fileapi/drivefs_async_file_util.cc;l=239-242;drc=b7fcea93b3ee24beb19e0bb2a5fbde4f83b484d1



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/drive/fileapi/drivefs_async_file_util.cc;l=239-242;drc=b7fcea93b3ee24beb19e0bb2a5fbde4f83b484d1"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/drive/fileapi/drivefs_async_file_util.cc;l=239-242;drc=b7fcea93b3ee24beb19e0bb2a5fbde4f83b484d1<!----></a>



<br>



<br>



<br>





This is unsafe because every time DriveFS mounted, PinManager instance would be recreated in |DriveIntegrationService::OnMounted| [1]. The previous PinManager instance might get destroyed before the scheduled task is executed. As a result, `PinManager::NotifyDelete` would access freed memory.



<span class="line"><!---->This is unsafe because every time DriveFS mounted, PinManager instance would be recreated in |DriveIntegrationService::OnMounted| [1]. The previous PinManager instance might get destroyed before the scheduled task is executed. As a result, `PinManager::NotifyDelete` would access freed memory.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





void DriveIntegrationService::OnMounted(const base::FilePath& mount_path) {



<span class="line"><!---->void DriveIntegrationService::OnMounted(const base::FilePath&amp; mount_path) {<!----></span>



<br>





  ...



<span class="line"><!---->  ...<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  if (ash::features::IsDriveFsBulkPinningEnabled()) {



<span class="line"><!---->  if (ash::features::IsDriveFsBulkPinningEnabled()) {<!----></span>



<br>





    pin_manager_ = std::make_unique<drivefs::pinning::PinManager>(



<span class="line"><!---->    pin_manager_ = std::make_unique&lt;drivefs::pinning::PinManager&gt;(<!----></span>



<br>





        profile_->GetPath(), GetDriveFsInterface());          // <---- [1]



<span class="line"><!---->        profile_-&gt;GetPath(), GetDriveFsInterface());          // &lt;---- [1]<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/drive/drive_integration_service.cc;l=1082;drc=3ddb2d68ccf2ff0f5b11064ad9ca58ba9ebe49bd



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/drive/drive_integration_service.cc;l=1082;drc=3ddb2d68ccf2ff0f5b11064ad9ca58ba9ebe49bd"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/drive/drive_integration_service.cc;l=1082;drc=3ddb2d68ccf2ff0f5b11064ad9ca58ba9ebe49bd<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chromeos/ash/components/drivefs/drivefs_pin_manager.cc;l=841-853;drc=aac51605c2403af35ddf6f73d47c860a0ba4e5ba



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chromeos/ash/components/drivefs/drivefs_pin_manager.cc;l=841-853;drc=aac51605c2403af35ddf6f73d47c860a0ba4e5ba"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chromeos/ash/components/drivefs/drivefs_pin_manager.cc;l=841-853;drc=aac51605c2403af35ddf6f73d47c860a0ba4e5ba<!----></a>



<br>



<br>



<br>





After some digging around in the source code, it looks like the DriveFS can be remounted.



<span class="line"><!---->After some digging around in the source code, it looks like the DriveFS can be remounted.<!----></span>



<br>





1. Settings page -> Files -> Disconnect Google Drive account, toggle this option several times will cause DriveFS remounted.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Settings page -&gt; Files -&gt; Disconnect Google Drive account, toggle this option several times will cause DriveFS remounted.<!----></span>



<br>





2. In the webui chrome://drive-internals/, run chrome.send("restartDrive") in console or click "Restart Drive" button.



<span class="line"><!---->2. In the webui chrome://drive-internals/, run chrome.send("restartDrive") in console or click "Restart Drive" button.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: head



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: head<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: ChromeOS



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: ChromeOS<!----></span>



<br>





CL: 



<span class="line"><!---->CL: <!----></span>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4216533



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4216533"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4216533<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





This problem was found by code review and DriveFS is not avaiable for me. However, I think following steps can reproduce the problem reliably.



<span class="line"><!---->This problem was found by code review and DriveFS is not avaiable for me. However, I think following steps can reproduce the problem reliably.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Apply drivefs_async_file_util.patch, which adds sleep(10) in the DeleteOperation::Delete function running on IO thread



<span class="line"><!---->1. Apply drivefs_async_file_util.patch, which adds sleep(10) in the DeleteOperation::Delete function running on IO thread<!----></span>



<br>





2. Visit the attach test.html page, click and select a directory from DriveFS. Or delete a test directory in drive fs manually.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Visit the attach test.html page, click and select a directory from DriveFS. Or delete a test directory in drive fs manually.<!----></span>



<br>





3. In 10 seconds, open page chrome://drive-internals/, run chrome.send("restartDrive") in console or click "Restart Drive" button.



<span class="line"><!---->3. In 10 seconds, open page chrome://drive-internals/, run chrome.send("restartDrive") in console or click "Restart Drive" button.<!----></span>



<br>





4. Wait the task run and UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->4. Wait the task run and UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Steps without patch, may not work:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps without patch, may not work:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Open page chrome://drive-internals/, run in console: f = function() {  chrome.send('restartDrive'); setTimeout(f, 1000);}; f()



<span class="line"><!---->1. Open page chrome://drive-internals/, run in console: f = function() {  chrome.send('restartDrive'); setTimeout(f, 1000);}; f()<!----></span>



<br>





2. Visit the attach test.html page, click and select a directory from DriveFS.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Visit the attach test.html page, click and select a directory from DriveFS.<!----></span>

Hello Chaobin Zhang (OP), when submitting security bugs, thanks for your attempts to assist here, but please do not endeavor to add and adjust security labels. All security bugs should go through security triage by the appropriate security team. Security labels impact our security and release processes and should be set by Chrome browser or ChromeOS security sheriffs. Thank you for your assistance!



<span class="line"><!---->Hello Chaobin Zhang (OP), when submitting security bugs, thanks for your attempts to assist here, but please do not endeavor to add and adjust security labels. All security bugs should go through security triage by the appropriate security team. Security labels impact our security and release processes and should be set by Chrome browser or ChromeOS security sheriffs. Thank you for your assistance!<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
